# Tier D ground truth: AquaScan 'N' (new-files scan) — captured 2026-07-03 from the
# live FS-UAE reference board (docker amiexpress-ref) by comparison/harness/ae_tierd_newfiles.py.

# PASS 1 (discovery): the dirs sub-prompt was unknown, so every prompted scenario
# answered Enter=None at 'Directories: ... (Enter)=None ?' and aborted before scanning.
# Pass 1 is kept because it uniquely proves the date prompt's default is the DAY OF
# LAST CALL: it shows (Enter)=06-25-26 while the connect banner says today is 03-Jul-2026
# (last call was Thu 25-Jun-2026). It also holds the first captures of the N help screen,
# inline N 01-01-26 / N -30, and 'N R -1' -> Argument error!.
#
# PASS 2 (definitive): same day, second session — last call is now earlier today, so the
# default date shows 07-03-26. Answers both prompts everywhere; covers every verb of the
# 'N ?' grammar, the money capture (01-01-26 x All dirs paged to the end), reverse, quick
# scan, non-stop, !x newest, T/Y/S tokens, error envelopes, and the empty conference.
